CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS Tecmis;
USE Tecmis;

CREATE TABLE USER (
    Username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    First_Name VARCHAR(50),
    Last_Name VARCHAR(50) ,
    Role VARCHAR(50),
    Phone_Number VARCHAR(15),
    Email VARCHAR(100),
    Password VARCHAR(255),
    Profile_Pic_Path VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE Admin (
    Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY
);
CREATE TABLE Lecturer (
    Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY
    
);

CREATE TABLE Technical_officer (
    Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY
   
);

CREATE TABLE Timetable (
    Timetable_id CHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
    Username VARCHAR(50),
    Content LONGTEXT
    
);

CREATE TABLE Student (
    Username VARCHAR(50) PRIMARY KEY,
    Timetable_id CHAR(10)
   
);

CREATE TABLE Course_unit (
    Course_code CHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
    CourseName VARCHAR(100),
    Course_type VARCHAR(20),
    Theory_hours INT ,
    Practical_hours INT ,
    Credits INT,
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Admin_Username VARCHAR(50)
    
);

CREATE TABLE Student_course_unit (
    Username VARCHAR(50),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Username, Course_code)
    
);


CREATE TABLE Medical (
    Medical_id CHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
    Submission_date VARCHAR(15),
    Status VARCHAR(15),
    Start_date  VARCHAR(15),
    End_date VARCHAR(15),
    Reason VARCHAR(100),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Medical_image VARCHAR(255)
    
);



CREATE TABLE Attendance (
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Session_Type VARCHAR(15) ,
    Session_date VARCHAR(50) ,
    Status VARCHAR(15),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Student_Username,Course_code,Session_Type,Session_date)
);

CREATE TABLE Lecturer_Attendance (
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Lecturer_Username,Student_Username,Course_code)
);


CREATE TABLE Marks (
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Course_code CHAR(10),
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    Quiz1 FLOAT ,
    Quiz2 FLOAT ,
    Quiz3 FLOAT ,
    Quiz4 FLOAT ,
    Assessment_01 FLOAT,
    Assessment_02 FLOAT,
    Mid_Practical FLOAT ,
    Mid_Theory FLOAT ,
    End_Practical FLOAT ,
    End_Theory FLOAT ,
    PRIMARY KEY (Student_Username, Course_code)
    
);


CREATE TABLE Lecturer_Medical (
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Medical_id CHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (Lecturer_Username,Medical_id)
);
CREATE TABLE Timetable_TO_Officer (
    Timetable_id CHAR(10),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Timetable_id,TO_Username)
);


CREATE TABLE Notice (
    Notice_id CHAR(10) PRIMARY KEY,
    Title VARCHAR(50),
    Publish_date VARCHAR(50),
    Admin_Username VARCHAR(50),
    Content TEXT NOT NULL,
    Category VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
    Attachment VARCHAR(1000)
    
);

CREATE TABLE Notice_Lecturer (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    Lecturer_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id, Lecturer_Username)
    
);

CREATE TABLE Notice_Student (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    Student_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id, Student_Username)
    
);
CREATE TABLE Notice_TO_Officer (
    Notice_id CHAR(10),
    TO_Username VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (Notice_id, TO_Username)
    
);



/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
ALTER TABLE Admin
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Username) REFERENCES USER(Username); 

ALTER TABLE Lecturer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Username) REFERENCES USER(Username); 

ALTER TABLE Technical_officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Username) REFERENCES USER(Username);

ALTER TABLE Timetable
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Username) REFERENCES Admin(Username);

ALTER TABLE Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Username) REFERENCES USER(Username);

ALTER TABLE Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Timetable_id) REFERENCES Timetable(Timetable_id);

ALTER TABLE Course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Username);

ALTER TABLE Course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Admin_Username) REFERENCES Admin(Username);

ALTER TABLE Student_course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Username) REFERENCES Student(Username);

ALTER TABLE Student_course_unit
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Username);


ALTER TABLE Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(Username);
 
ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Username);


ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(Username);

ALTER TABLE Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Medical_id) REFERENCES Medical(Medical_id);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Username);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Username);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Attendance
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Username);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Username);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Course_code) REFERENCES Course_unit(Course_code);

ALTER TABLE Marks
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Medical_id) REFERENCES Medical(Medical_id) ;

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Username);

ALTER TABLE Lecturer_Medical
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Medical_id) REFERENCES Medical(Medical_id);

ALTER TABLE Timetable_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(Username);

ALTER TABLE Timetable_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Timetable_id) REFERENCES Timetable(Timetable_id);


ALTER TABLE Notice
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Admin_Username) REFERENCES Admin(Username);


ALTER TABLE Notice_Lecturer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Notice_id) REFERENCES Notice(Notice_id);

ALTER TABLE Notice_Lecturer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Lecturer_Username) REFERENCES Lecturer(Username); 

ALTER TABLE Notice_Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Notice_id) REFERENCES Notice(Notice_id);

ALTER TABLE Notice_Student
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Student_Username) REFERENCES Student(Username);

ALTER TABLE Notice_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (Notice_id) REFERENCES Notice(Notice_id);

ALTER TABLE Notice_TO_Officer
ADD FOREIGN KEY (TO_Username) REFERENCES Technical_officer(Username);

CREATE TABLE Course_Materials (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    course_code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    lecturer_no VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
